</span><span class="x1lliihq">    # Calculate temperature based on time using the quadratic equation
</span><span class="x1lliihq">    temperature = a * time**2 + b * time + c
</span><span class="x1lliihq">    return temperature
</span><span class="x1lliihq">

</span><span class="x1lliihq">
